  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8d90d091-404e-4aec-86c5-3a299d632018'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

  <span id="freeText420516003496524964" style="display:none">He saw her first, but his friend made the move.<br /><br />She settled for the safer choice, but her heart knew the truth.<br /><br />They love, they crave, they lie.<br /><br />Garrett McCarthy, Annabelle Parker, and Milo Roberts were as close as friends could get. They shared in each other's joy during graduations, promotions, and engagements. They consoled one another through heartache and loss.<br /><br />When one of the friend's life is tragically cut short, it's up to the two left behind to pick up the pieces and find out the truth - no matter the cost. As they slowly start to uncover the nature of his deception, and the very powerful people behind it, they begin to question everyone and everything, even themselves.<br /><br />Everyone has secrets - some do it for love while others do it for power. Those secrets can change perceptions, alter reality and sometimes destroy lives.<br /><br />What do you do when you find out your whole life has been a lie?</span>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_483280393" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/483280393" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/483280393?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews?shelf=january-2013">january-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483280393" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14083237197860920084"><b>Your first MUST read of 2013...</b><br/><br/>Call me a cynic, but my expectations of this book were...I tried not to have any. How can you go from one literary extreme to another? How? Why?<br/><br/>So before reading <i>A Beautiful Lie</i> I hailed Mary, lit a candle, threw some salt, kissed a baby, and gave myself the "you <i>will</i> love this" pep talk. Fail! I did <b>not</b> love <i>A Beautiful Lie</i>. Nope...I more than loved it! I fell so hard I hit something I didn't see coming. I hit something great. T.E. Sivec is able to exist on both e</span>
  <span id="freeText14083237197860920084" style="display:none"><b>Your first MUST read of 2013...</b><br /><br />Call me a cynic, but my expectations of this book were...I tried not to have any. How can you go from one literary extreme to another? How? Why?<br /><br />So before reading <i>A Beautiful Lie</i> I hailed Mary, lit a candle, threw some salt, kissed a baby, and gave myself the "you <i>will</i> love this" pep talk. Fail! I did <b>not</b> love <i>A Beautiful Lie</i>. Nope...I more than loved it! I fell so hard I hit something I didn't see coming. I hit something great. T.E. Sivec is able to exist on both ends of the spectrum and she does this flawlessly. <br /><br />The third person took some getting use to, but it won me over and I loved it. I was given insight to both Garrett and Parker in every situation. It made me feel a connect with the characters that got under my skin; it gave the book life. I was allowed to see how their relationship developed from the very beginning, but at the same time the story progressed. It was the perfect amount of friendship, tension, passion, and love. I can not tell you how much this made me fall in love with...with everything. Made me fall in love with Garrett. Garrett who instantly became one of my favorite male characters of all time. He made my vagina want to jump inside the pages! He made my heart beat faster and defined what it means to be perfect. Everything about him was perfect. <br /><br />I devour Kristen Ashley books like their crack!!! I love her strong alpha characters and her extreme action packed storylines. ABL took those elements, but took it to a new level; it's own level. <br /><br />The intimate scenes were hot and passionate without being cheesy; there was no unrealistic during sex banter that made me cringe. Just a simple guttural “fuck” said it all. The “almost” sex scenes were almost hotter than the actual moment. Raw passion. <br /><br />Of course with any book you love, you never want it to end. But at the same time, the author did a beautiful job giving me everything I needed from this book. I had closure; I was able to <i>let</i> it end. Parker and Garrett didn’t need a sequel, but that didn't stop me from going back and re-reading my favorite moments over...and over...and over again. It stayed with me for days. It's still with me.<br /><br />I feel like I’ve been reading the same book over and over again lately. T.E. Sivec has brought something new, something intense, something passionate, and something bad ass to the table. Intense circumstances are the best aphrodisiacs; this book was one giant aphrodisiac! This book pulled me in, took me on a ride, and made me fall in love! I’m pretty sure T.E. Sivec is soon to become synonymous with intense passion, romance, and bad assness! Be careful when you touch this book...IT'S HOT!<br /><br />READ ON!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14083237197860920084" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

I loved it. It has been lying <br/>on my kindle for a couple of months - not sure why I had not read it before this.<br/>It is a story about friendship, love, betrayal, loyalty, <br/>life, death - it has it all. But is their friendship based on truth or lies?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380747705i/3118850._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>… if you were given the chance to go back, to tell the truth<br> instead of lie to save someone's life and their feelings... would you? <br><br>Two best friends fall for the same girl. They had been through so much together, childhood, college, Navy Seal training….<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380747705i/3118851._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Garrett and Milo are Navy Seals. He has loved her for years but because of his loyalty to Milo,he has never acted on it, not even now that Milo is dead. <br>They must pose as a married couple ....<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380747705i/3118852.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Let's just say that it wasn't just the temperature in the <br>Dominican Republic that was HOT, Garrett and Parker could <br>sure spin a hot scene once they got going. <br>Won't go into all the details about the rest of the book - <br>will leave it to your goodselves to read it and judge. <br>I paid $4.40 for it and I see that it is now on sale on Amazon for 64 cents. <br>A BARGAIN - GO AND BUY IT.<br><br>AND yes, happily for lil' old me they did get ….<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380747705i/3118853.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>"This one day, a sweet, beautiful girl walked into a coffee shop<br>and my world came to a standstill. <br>She was shy and had a smile that could light up a room. <br>But there was something in her eyes that made me want to <br>take away all of her pain. I couldn't breathe, I couldn't speak … <br>I just wanted to know her. But I had a friend who had a rough life. <br>He was always getting pushed aside and struggling to be happy. <br>I saw him make that beautiful girl laugh, <br>and I knew I needed to step back. <br>I knew I needed to let him grab onto that happiness once and for all. <br>I stepped aside and I watched them grow together <br>and love together and each and every moment it tore my heart in two. <br>I wanted it to be me. I wanted to be the one to love her. <br>So I did. <br>She just never knew it…. <br>when something you've wanted for as long as you can remember is finally yours, you can have a hard time believing it's real.<br>You find yourself wondering if it's just a dream and<br>in one careless moment it will all be taken away from you ...."</i><br><br><br>Sigh, I loved Garrett.<br><br>"I love you." ….. And in time she knew all of her wounds would heal as long as she had Garrett to love her.<br><br><br>…. And I get my Epilogue - seriously, every book should have an Epilogue …..<br><br><pre>Garrett realised in that moment<br>it was time to say goodbye to the past <br>and the beautiful lies he'd told and<br>say hello to his future.</pre><br><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16085614.A_Beautiful_Lie__Playing_with_Fire___1_" title="A Beautiful Lie (Playing with Fire, #1) by Tara Sivec" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_436347826" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/436347826" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/436347826?book_show_action=true">Oct 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer436347826" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10634548123449691672">I am so impressed! As much as I love Tara Sivec’s Chocolate Lovers series(some of the funniest books I have ever read!) This book is in a whole different league! It is AMAZING! This book had a little comedy, romance and tons of action, suspense and steam! I loved it!!!<br/><br/><b>
  <i>But if you were given the chance to go back, to tell the truth instead of lie to save someones life and their feelings... would you?</i>
</b><br/><br/>Parker and Garrett have been best friends for eight years. They have always had feelings for ea</span>
  <span id="freeText10634548123449691672" style="display:none">I am so impressed! As much as I love Tara Sivec’s Chocolate Lovers series(some of the funniest books I have ever read!) This book is in a whole different league! It is AMAZING! This book had a little comedy, romance and tons of action, suspense and steam! I loved it!!!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>But if you were given the chance to go back, to tell the truth instead of lie to save someones life and their feelings... would you?</i>
</b><br /><br />Parker and Garrett have been best friends for eight years. They have always had feelings for each other, a spark. Parker meets Garrett and Milo her first year of college. They are best friends. Although Garrett gives her butterflies and makes her hear race, Parker is afraid to pursue anything with Garrett from the very beginning. She ends up dating Milo, someone safe and uncomplicated. <br /><b>
  <i>She swore she would never let someone take so much of her heart and soul that it would wither away to nothing once they were gone. She gave up on the dream of finding someone to consume her mind, body, and soul. It only ruined you in the end. It left you broken and unable to live.<br />He was the one person that could make her change her mind about everything and it scared her to death. </i>
</b><br />Garrett loves Parker, but he never acts on it because Milo has been his best friend since he's been a kid. He has always been there for Milo to protect him and defend him. He assumes Milo and Parker are happy, good for each other, and in love. He would never interfere with his two best friends relationship. <br /><br />Garrett and Milo are both Navy Seals. Parker is an accomplished photographer. Parker and Milo are engaged to be married. Then one day, Milo gets killed during a secret mission to the Dominican. Things look suspicious so Garrett volunteers to check things out... Parker goes with him. She has some secrets of her own. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[She is a really a badass CIA agent <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />They take a team there, and try to uncover some truth to what has happened to Milo...<br /><i>
  <b>He’d been one person with Garrett and another with Parker. And obviously, he’d been a third person with both of them. Garrett had no idea which Milo was the real one.</b>
</i><br />I would love to go into this book, but I don’t want to give too much away- I was shocked when a lot of things came to light, especially in the end. Parker and Garrett discover so much about each other that they never knew. Obviously, with Milo out of the picture... they start to explore there feelings for one another. <br /><b>
  <i>“But he doesn’t look at you like he just wants to be friends, little ninja. He looks at you like you’re the key to his soul and like he wants to devour you.”</i>
</b><br />The ‘almost’ sex scenes and the sex scenes in this book were passionate and hot... crazy hot! <br /><br />I fell in love with Garrett in this book! He is such a great guy, he’s kind, loyal, protective, sexy and just completely lovable. I also really like Parker a lot. She was a tough cookie and I was really shocked with what came to be with her character. I connected with both of them and loved the chemistry between them. Milo... <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I wasn’t so shocked when I found out he was alive, but holy crap... mother of all deception! I was so surprised with what happened with him! Ultimate betrayal with Parker and Garrett, his only real family. I was disgusted with him. I mostly felt heartbroken for Garrett and Parker. How much of the last eight(much longer for Garrett) years of their lives with Milo were real and what was fake <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I was hooked from the beginning of this story. I loved everything about it! I don't read a lot of third person pov's, but it was cool to see a little bit inside of everyones head. It had more action then I’m used to, but a lot of heart also. It kept me on my toes... but it also made me smile, made me cry <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Oh the letter from her dad... cried like a baby! <b><i> The truth is, you’re mother wasn’t the love of my life, not really. She was my wife, and I always have and always will love her. But you, my Annabelle, my daughter, YOU are the love of my life. </i></b> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> it was just awesome! Take a chance on this book! It doesn’t matter what genre you are used to reading, its got a little something for everyone! <br /><br />Some of my favorite quotes: (possible spoilers... reader beware :D Garrett is so fantastic! )<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I shouldn’t have waited until I almost lost you. I know love isn’t something that comes easy for you or that you even believe in it. I know and I don’t care. I don’t care if you’re afraid to love me back, I don’t care if you never feel the same way I do. I just need you to know, right here and right now, that I am in love with you, Annabelle Parker.”<br /><br />“I’m not scared because I can’t give you my love in return, I’m scared because I love you so much sometimes its hard to breathe. I’m scared because I never wanted to lose myself in someone as deeply as my parents did. I’m scared because I was so stupid to realize I would have no control over that where you were concerned.”<br /><br />“When something you’ve wanted for as long as you can remember is finally yours, you have a hard time believing its real. You find yourself wondering if it’s just a dream and in one careless moment it will all be taken away from you.”<br /><br />It symbolized their past, present, and future. It represented the fact that through it all, the love they shared could heal even the most severe wounds. <br /><br />All of the pain, all of the longing and regrets, every single moment was worth it in the end. If he’d made different choices back then, if he’d told the truth and made her his, they might not be where they are right now. </i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="10634548123449691672" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_468438594" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/468438594" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/468438594?book_show_action=true">Dec 02, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer468438594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1954014864020661720">This is a really hard review for me because I didn't really want to feel the way I did about this book, but I'm going to just be 100% honest here. I adored the Chocolate Lovers series. And I wanted to love this book. I really, truly did. With all my heart. But… this book was not really for me in the end. I ended up sort of liking it, but really not connecting to it in any emotional way – which, to me, is a huge part of what I seek when I read a book.<br/><br/>I should start off by saying that one of the r</span>
  <span id="freeText1954014864020661720" style="display:none">This is a really hard review for me because I didn't really want to feel the way I did about this book, but I'm going to just be 100% honest here. I adored the Chocolate Lovers series. And I wanted to love this book. I really, truly did. With all my heart. But… this book was not really for me in the end. I ended up sort of liking it, but really not connecting to it in any emotional way – which, to me, is a huge part of what I seek when I read a book.<br><br>I should start off by saying that one of the reasons I loved the Chocolate Lovers series was not just because they were funny, but because they also had a bit of a bit of heart and I really cared for the characters.<br><br>I didn’t find that with this book though. I felt that the writing style ‘told’ me the story rather than allowing me to ‘experience’ it and as such I felt a bit of a disconnect from the characters.<br><br>This is a story about Navy Seals, secret missions, and the requiting of an unrequited love.<br>When there are suspicious circumstances surrounding the death of their best friend Milo, its up to Garrett and Annabelle to go back to his last known location and figure out the truth behind it.<br>But when they go undercover as a couple, how long can they hold up the pretense before their real feelings start to take over?<br><br><i> "The way they argued, the way they joked, the way they loved, the way they took care of one another - it all boiled down to the fact that they were just meant to be together like this." </i><br><br>I’m going to admit that I feel pretty bad giving this book a 3 star rating but, in the interest of full honesty, I don’t feel I can give it more. However, I will say that it is a happy, full 3. This is not a bad book at all, there were just a lot of elements to it that didn’t make me 'feel' for and be emotionally connected to the story which kept me from rating it higher: the narrative that told rather than showed, the lack of communication and self-imposed UST between the main characters (seriously, I just wanted to lock them in a room and not let them out till their had told each other the truth) drove me a little crazy, and there were a few things that make me look at the page with squinty skeptical eyes. But also, again in the interest of honesty here, I think maybe it might the genre? After reading this book and a few others like it, I don’t honestly think that romantic suspense is my thing. I guess at the end of the day, I prefer more character driven stories where its focused more on the emotional connection with and to the characters than it is about the details of the plot.<br><br>Now, this being said, the plot of this book was exciting and engaging in many places and I was interested in it. There were a few steamy scenes - especially the whole 'pool' thing!! Hot! And I also enjoyed how the deeper they dug into the situation, the more the mystery deepened.<br><br>But, I don’t know. I guess I just really wasn’t feeling that ‘spark’ with this book.<br><br>This being said, I’m still a huge fan of Tara’s writing and am looking forward to her next book. She tells a good story and since this is her first foray into a new genre, I have no doubt that the books will just keep getting better and better.<br><br>My casting:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399501i/773182.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399501i/773183._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Back cover:<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380399501i/773184._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="1954014864020661720" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText17227755860628302804" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>4.5 Action packed and Sexified Stars</i>
</b><br><br><b>OKay.. Seriously They are Perfect!!!!!! </b><br><br>My Cast:<br><br>Garrett is played by Henry Cavill<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379769120i/275086._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Parker is played by Olivia Wilde<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398357i/769781._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Milo played by Adam Rodriguez <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398357i/769782._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book should be made into a movie.. Immediately. <br><br>Seriously.<br>Someone needs to get on that like right down- Mark my words. The movie would be a freakin hit!<br><br>A Beautiful Lie was not what I expected. I admit I didnt do much research about it, I didnt even read other reviews... I honestly just jumped head first into this beautiful story.<br><br>I was pleasantly surprised.<br><br>I was getting into a bit of a book funk and this cured it.<br><br>The heroine was a beautiful woman with spunk to match. She was fierce and powerful and could take care of herself.. You gotta love a female character that is seriously bad effin ass. And Parker was definitely that.<br><br>The main man, or as I like to call him <b>my new husband</b>, Garrett, was the hottest thing. Lord. He was down right sexy with his love for Parker and wanting nothing more than to be with her but keeping his feelings from her because his best friend was "in love" with her. The fact that he was a military man just made him that much hotter to me. *fans self*. <br><br>The story was rich with action. Twists and Turns were spewing from every direction and half the time I had no idea what would happen next. <br><br>I fell in love with Parker and Garrett and wanted to jump into the fighting scenes and kick some serious ass every time there was a fight!<br><br>Read this book ya'll! :) </span>

Most people on here seem to be between 2-4 stars for it. Me personally. LOVE IT!</b></span>

<div id="review_505508566" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/505508566" />
    <a title="Karla" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3117503-karla"><img alt="Karla" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383769554p2/3117503.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/505508566?book_show_action=true">Jan 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Karla" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Karla" href="/user/show/3117503-karla">Karla</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer505508566" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13132174930122328116">This book just started off all wrong for me. I really need to start reading the samples before relying on the average review rating to buy a book:<br/><br/>1.	One of my absolute biggest pet peeves of writing – third person omniscient. When done well, I don’t mind it – but in this book, the head jumps are just too frequent. From one paragraph to another, it’s disorienting to jump between that many points of view. (I think I could have been okay with switching POV between sections or chapters, but not withi</span>
  <span id="freeText13132174930122328116" style="display:none">This book just started off all wrong for me. I really need to start reading the samples before relying on the average review rating to buy a book:<br /><br />1.	One of my absolute biggest pet peeves of writing – third person omniscient. When done well, I don’t mind it – but in this book, the head jumps are just too frequent. From one paragraph to another, it’s disorienting to jump between that many points of view. (I think I could have been okay with switching POV between sections or chapters, but not within the same scene.) I found myself struggling to get through the first few chapters to even make it to the story.<br /><br />2.	Spoon-fed information whenever the author felt like it. Character and story development relied on quasi flashbacks to whatever relevant period of time to provide background. They weren’t well placed, and actually disrupted the flow of the story.<br /><br />3.	I didn’t realize this was some kind of Navy Seal / CIA thriller. If I had, I would have either (a) passed, or (b) found a novel written by an author familiar with the genre. Either way, I bought the book, so I muddled through it. I’m no expert on how Navy Seals and the CIA do things, but I had to suspend disbelief in a couple of areas that seemed so simple:<br /><br />a.	I doubt that, while going deep undercover, a trained CIA agent would carry identifying information for her actual identity. (At one point, she whips out her passport to show the other main character that she worked for the CIA)<br /><br /> b.	Not sure why a highly complex mission with elite members would wait until they were onsite to do background/internet research on their targets. <br /><br />The story was interesting enough, but I found myself distracted by the writing style. Mostly personal preference, but frustrating none the less. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13132174930122328116" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/502988925?book_show_action=true">Jan 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fathima" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fathima" href="/user/show/5799807-fathima">Fathima</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5799807-fathima?shelf=my-fav-author">my-fav-author</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5799807-fathima?shelf=cover-love">cover-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer502988925" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9034397918076246846"><a href='http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&current=Beautifullies.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404648i/787640.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"When something you’ve wanted for as long as you can remember is finally yours, you have a hard time believing it’s real,” Garrett said softly as he moved closer to Parker and her body angled towards him. “You find yourself wondering if it’s just a dream and in one careless moment it will all be taken away from you.” </i>
</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&current=Couplelove.jpg' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404648i/787641.jpg' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Woohoo ! Tara Sivec really twists a 360 with this one !! From her hugely acclaimed , laugh-your-ass-out comedy 'The Chocolate Lovers - <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704001.Seduction_and_Snacks__Chocolate_Lovers___1_' title='Seduction and Snacks (Chocolate Lovers, #1) by Tara Sivec' rel='nofollow noopener'>Seduction and Snacks</a> <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15769463.Futures_and_Frosting__Chocolate_Lovers___2_' title='Futures and Frosting (Chocolate Lovers, #2) by Tara Sivec' rel='nofollow noopener'>Futures and F</a></span>
  <span id="freeText9034397918076246846" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Beautifullies.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404648i/787640.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"When something you’ve wanted for as long as you can remember is finally yours, you have a hard time believing it’s real,” Garrett said softly as he moved closer to Parker and her body angled towards him. “You find yourself wondering if it’s just a dream and in one careless moment it will all be taken away from you.” </i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Couplelove.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404648i/787641.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Woohoo ! Tara Sivec really twists a 360 with this one !! From her hugely acclaimed , laugh-your-ass-out comedy 'The Chocolate Lovers - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15704001.Seduction_and_Snacks__Chocolate_Lovers___1_" title="Seduction and Snacks (Chocolate Lovers, #1) by Tara Sivec" rel="nofollow noopener">Seduction and Snacks</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/15769463.Futures_and_Frosting__Chocolate_Lovers___2_" title="Futures and Frosting (Chocolate Lovers, #2) by Tara Sivec" rel="nofollow noopener">Futures and Frosting</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16107588.Troubles_and_Treats__Chocolate_Lovers___3_" title="Troubles and Treats (Chocolate Lovers, #3) by Tara Sivec" rel="nofollow noopener">Troubles and Treats</a> ' series to an intelligent military styled romance , she's proved herself to be quite a versatile novelist ! <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Everybodylies.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404648i/787642._SX540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>A beautiful Lie basically revolves around 3 best friends , Garrett McCarthy , Annabelle Parker and Milo Roberts . 3 best friends who met each other when they were in college . Milo and Anna fell in love while Garrett always wished for their happiness . It didn't matter that he harbored feelings for Anna , for him the only thing that mattered was Milo's happiness . And Milo's happiness was Anna . So Garrett watched , pretended to be happy and always wished the best for his best friends . Anna wanted her heart to be safe . She did not want to fall in love with someone deeply . She did not want someone else to be able to break the walls around her heart or her heart . She did not want anybody else to have the power of love over her . So she chose the easy way out . Squashed her feelings for Garrett and accepted what Milo had to offer . Because Milo was much easier to handle . <br><br><i>Yo Garrett and Anna ... </i><br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=Yousureaboutthat.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404648ra/787643.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Well , moving on .....<br><br>Eight years later , things have changed . Changed to a whole lot of mess ! Milo is gone , leaving Garrett and Anna to pick up the pieces and move on . But nothing was as it seemed . Everyone has secrets . Everyone lies for their conveniences , for protecting someone they love , for getting something that has been denied to them for too long . Garrett and Anna want the truth , and nothing but the truth . Even if it meant uncovering their own lies to one another . <br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=liesandtruth.png" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380404648i/787644.png" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>But what will they find ?? What will they see when the clouds of deception and lies finally clear out the sky ??? Well , read the book and find out for yourself ..<br><br><b>
  <u> My thoughts : </u>
</b><br><br>Like I mentioned earlier , A beautiful Lie is a very cleverly etched story . The story moves back and forth giving the readers glimpses of Garrett , Anna and Milo's relationship and their history . T.E Sivec manages to keep the reader embroiled in this concrete web of deception and lies that , as a reader you cant help but ask ..<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=whay-is-happening.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380400524ra/776362.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i> yeah , I found myself asking me that question <b> a lot </b> of times ! </i><br><br>The characters are pretty likeable ! My favorite absolutely being Annabelle Parker ! That lady needs no man I tell ya ... She kicks asses and takes no prisoners ! Goooooooo<br><br><a href="http://s1171.photobucket.com/albums/r551/Fathima23/?action=view&amp;current=girlpower.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380404648ra/787645.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Absolutely loved her ! <br><br>Garrett really shined as the always sacrificing best friend ! Although , the guy is a total no-nonsense dude , he always did what he could for his best friends . And Milo , well ... Just Crazy ! Like Crazy with a capital C !!!! <br><br>The sexual tension in this book is over-the-rooftop hot ! Garrett and Anna wanted each other but thought about a lot of things , like a shit load of things to act upon their feelings ! All their almost-sex encounters were definitely burning down a few panties somewhere ! * wink wink * <br><br>To sum it all up , A beautiful lie is a grip-the-edge-of-your-seats story that will leave the reader feeling like they've just watched a top-notch Hollywood action film with all its glitz and glamor !<br><br>I cant wait to read more in the Playing With Fire series ! </span>
  <a data-text-id="9034397918076246846" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_482405044" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/482405044" />
    <a title="Paula " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2879703-paula"><img alt="Paula " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1536687412p2/2879703.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/482405044?book_show_action=true">Dec 21, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2879703-paula?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer482405044" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14636598569587085337"><br/>-- <i>A <a href='http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br/><br/><i>
  <b>It’s a beautiful lie. It’s the perfect denial. Such a beautiful lie to believe in.</b>
</i><b></b> <br/><br/>I really adore Tara Sivec’s Chocolate series but <i>A Beautiful</i> Lie shows just how eclectic and talented of a writer she truly is. I am honored and excited to be able to review this story for her. A Beautiful Lie starts off with a slow build, as the reader gets to know the characters and their past history. And, just when I was growing slightly bored of the character’s back story,</span>
  <span id="freeText14636598569587085337" style="display:none"><br />-- <i>A <a href="http://romanticbookaffairs.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Romantic Book Affairs</a> Review</i><br /><br /><i>
  <b>It’s a beautiful lie. It’s the perfect denial. Such a beautiful lie to believe in.</b>
</i><b></b> <br /><br />I really adore Tara Sivec’s Chocolate series but <i>A Beautiful</i> Lie shows just how eclectic and talented of a writer she truly is. I am honored and excited to be able to review this story for her. A Beautiful Lie starts off with a slow build, as the reader gets to know the characters and their past history. And, just when I was growing slightly bored of the character’s back story, I was thrust into a suspenseful story loaded with plot twists, betrayals, secrets, hot passion, smoldering sexual tension, lies, lies, and more lies. <br /><br /><i>A Beautiful Lie</i> is Annabelle Parker, Garrett McCarthy, and Milo Roberts story. Garrett and Milo have been friends since high school, where Garrett and his family took Milo in from a very violent home where he was abused by his father. Garrett and Milo may not have been blood but they were brothers in every other way. They went to college together and then became Navy Seals together. Garrett and Milo met Parker at a coffee shop one day. Garrett was immediately drawn to Parker, but Milo is the one who claimed her as his. Garrett, the loyal friend that he is, would’ve done anything for Milo, even let him claim the one girl that stole his heart at first glance. And, for the next eight years, these three were as close as best friends could be. While one had the girl, the other wished he had the girl.<br /><br />Eventually Milo and Parker became engaged to be married. As Parker was planning the wedding, Milo went on a mission to the Dominican Republic. But he never came back home. He died during this mission. Garrett, unable to get over his best friend’s death, is determined to reveal what really happened on the island. So he volunteered to go on another mission in the Dominican Republic. This mission requires a man and woman to pose as a married couple who are a journalists and photographer. Their mission is to get close to the President of the Dominican Republic to expose a scandal.<br /><br />Parker is a world famous freelance photographer. When she finds out the photographer that originally was supposed to go on the mission, couldn’t go. Parker, stubborn and determined, decides to take her place. Garrett wants to protect Parker and refuses to let her go. But there is something Garrett doesn’t know about Parker which leaves him with no choice but to take her with him. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"If you were mine, I would never be able to walk away from you. If you were mine, I'd worship every inch of your body with my hands, lips, and tongue. If you were mine, I wouldn't be able to stand in the same room as you without running my hands over your skin and tasting your lips. If you were mine..."</b>
</i> -Garrett<br /><br />From the beginning, we learn about Garrett and Parker’s feelings for one another that they have never told each other for eight years. For years he kept his feelings hidden from Parker, and for years he has tried to fill the emptiness and jealousy over Milo and Parker’s relationship with empty relationships. But, even as he struggles with his guilt and shame, because of his love for his best friend’s girl, the battle that has been raging inside him reaches a breaking point. His carefully built walls began to crumble. And eventually fall. <br /><br />Oh, but Garrett is not the only one who has been hiding his feelings all these years. Parker gave herself to Milo, but her heart always belonged to Garrett. However, after Milo’s death and working closely to Garrett, things between them begin to heat up. And, because Parker no longer had Milo to hide behind, she could no longer deny her feelings for Garrett. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>"I’m not scared because I can't give you my love in return she told him softly. I'm scared because I love you so much sometimes it's hard to breathe"</b>
</i> –Parker<br /><br />I really love Garrett and Parker. They truly are friends first and foremost. The emotional baggage they’ve both been carrying around all these years is painful and sad. As they both battle internally with their feelings, I was extremely frustrated. I wanted them to fess up to their feelings, rip their clothes off, and have hot and fiery sex! And, good lord, the sexual tension between these two was off the charts explosive! The “almost” sex scenes were just as intense and smoldering, if not more, as the actual sex scenes. Ms. Sivec definitely knows how write sexual tension to the point my whole body was lit up with excitement. <br /><br />Not only was the sexual tension incredible, but the mystery behind Milo’s death was also incredibly intense. There are so many secrets and lies and betrayals all tightly woven into the plot. All of these characters have so many secrets. None of them could’ve ever imagined how different their lives would be after this mission. The plot twists were clever and would sneak up on me. I had quite a few “OMG” moments as I began to realize everything is not what it truly seems. Not to mention all of the “what if” moments. What if Garrett stepped forward and claimed Parker first? What if Parker decided not to date Milo? What if? What if? What if? <br /><br />To sum it up, this story is about how appearances can be deceiving, lies hurt, secrets hurt, and true love is unconditional. This exciting and engaging story kept me on the edge of my seat almost the entire time. The only thing that kept me from rating this book an A is the slow beginning. But if you struggle like I did at first, keep going, it is well worth it. I can’t wait to see what Ms. Sivec comes up with next in her new Playing with Fire series.<br /><br />Rating:B+<br />Heat: Hot<br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Find us on <a href="https://twitter.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> and <a href="http://facebook.com/rombookaffairs" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> too!</i>
</b><br /><br /></span>

<div id="review_482072346" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/482072346" />
    <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog"><img alt="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1554795448p2/3870376.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/482072346?book_show_action=true">Dec 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenny - TotallybookedBlog" href="/user/show/3870376-jenny---totallybookedblog">Jenny - TotallybookedBlog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer482072346" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5552102405929357559">This and other reviews can be found at <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://totallybookedblog.com/'>http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br/><br/><i>4.5 Stars</i><br/><br/>I have to honest and say when I initially picked this book up I went into it with reservations. Not about T E Sivec’s (Tara Sivec) talent because I had loved her Chocolate Series and know she can write wonderful characters and engaging stories, but this book about Navy Seals, which has suspense, romance and drama was such a departure from her previous work I did wonder how she was going to pull it off.<br/><br/>Well how misplaced</span>
  <span id="freeText5552102405929357559" style="display:none">This and other reviews can be found at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://totallybookedblog.com/">http://totallybookedblog.com/</a><br /><br /><i>4.5 Stars</i><br /><br />I have to honest and say when I initially picked this book up I went into it with reservations. Not about T E Sivec’s (Tara Sivec) talent because I had loved her Chocolate Series and know she can write wonderful characters and engaging stories, but this book about Navy Seals, which has suspense, romance and drama was such a departure from her previous work I did wonder how she was going to pull it off.<br /><br />Well how misplaced were those concerns and how clueless was I to ever question if she could do this! There is no doubt in my mind that this author nailed this genre! This book had it all. It was intriguing, romantic, suspenseful and not only that but this felt like more than a story, this book was like an adventure on pages and it was a journey I was on all the way!<br /><br />The story does build quite slowly at first while we’re introduced to the main characters Annabelle (Parker), Garrett (be still my book boyfriend heart!) and Milo and acquire background detail on their story. Three friends who are as close as friends could get. These three have an unbreakable bond. They’ve shared and experienced so much together and you really feel the camaraderie between them.<br /><br />I loved the characters of Parker and Garrett instantly. I connected with them and I was invested in these two from the very first page. I liked Milo, but he didn’t have the same pull for me that the other two did.<br /><br />I know the third person writing can be a distraction for some people but I never felt it in this book at all. I felt the moments and I loved the switch between Parker and Garrett which allowed me to see both sides of the story and therefore feel an all round connection with what was going on around them.<br /><br />Parker has to be up there as one of my favourite book heroines. This girl has it all. She’s confident, kick ass, full of personality, is strong yet incredibly vulnerable at same time. There are times I just wanted to give her a big. This girl really does get put through the wringer. What a wonderfully refreshing female character Parker was.<br /><br />I loved the way the story unfolded, I loved the flashbacks which gave us glimpses into their pasts and I was left positively gasping in parts due to the pure suspense of the story. Talk about getting the adrenaline pumping! I have to be honest and say I haven’t read many suspense stories, but if this is anything to go by I need to venture out more because this one definitely kept me on my toes.<br /><br />I was there every step of the way, I went everywhere they went, I saw it through their eyes and I felt everything they felt and at times it left me breathless!<br /><br />I was astounded at the level of detail T E Sivec brought to this book. It floored me how realistic the scenarios were that played out before my eyes. I’m guessing a lot of research went into writing this story.<br /><br />Be sure to dust off a spot on the book boyfriend shelf ladies because Garrett McCarthy is going to steal your heart! This alpha, hot Navy Seal definitely had me fanning myself on more than a few occasions. If I was ever caught in a dangerous situation this is the guy I want by my side. Oh hell, even if I wasn’t in a dangerous situation I’d want Garret beside me!<br /><br />Did I forget to mention the steam factor in this book? Yep, it’s pretty steamy that’s for sure, but the sex scenes aren’t contrived and felt real. They were passionate, romantic and hot indeed with the chemistry and sexual tension making me anticipate every moment.<br /><br />As I said before, this story is a slow burner and I urge you to hang on and strap yourself in because once it takes flight you will eventually be taken on a ride through some intense, suspenseful, emotional, dramatic and passionate scenes, in a story that I hope will bring as much to you as it did me.<br /><br />The conclusion was perfect, the epilogue was beautiful and I even shed a few tears. All in all this was an enjoyable reading experience.<br /><br /> <br /><br /><i>ARC supplied for an honest review</i></span>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer11952091161999222496"><b>Ok ,I think I'm finally ready....</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458959710ra/18553627.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>So I'll admit, At the beginning, I found this book utterly bored me out.   <span id="freeText11952091161999222496" style="display:none"><b>Ok ,I think I'm finally ready....</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458959710ra/18553627.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So I'll admit, At the beginning, I found this book utterly bored me out. The plot-line dragged on with the whole cliche <i>'I-love-my best-friend's-girl.Damn ! I wish I could have her !'</i> theme which kinda had Garrett (our tortured male lead ) wallowing in self pity for over 1/2 the book.There was honestly a point when I wondered if I'm ever going to find this book bearable enough to finish it. But I Forced myself to sit down and follow through.Not me babe I'm not a quitter.<br><br><b>
  <u> A Beautiful Lie by T.E.Sivec </u>
</b> is solely based on relationships between <b><i>Garrett McCarthy, Annabelle Parker, and Milo Roberts </i>.</b><br><br><i>All 3 best friends who stood together through thick and thin,all 3 best friends that ended up creating the most dangerous love triangle of all times....</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1458959710i/18553628.jpg" width="365" height="367" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The first 1/2 of the book was a total drag with the plot elaborating on the integrity of the NAVYSEALS and the CIA while on the other side droned on and on about Garrett's Self pity and guilt to such an extent.<i>I</i> was ready to take a gun and put it through <i>my </i> head,to end both our miseries.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450889066ra/17481542.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>(I honestly was in half a mind to throw them both into a life boat and leave them stranded all night until they worked their issues out..Serious communication problems are so over done.)</i><br><br>And Finally...Finally ! When I reached page 220;Things really started to pick up! Garrett and Annabelle,both moved down a step while the secondary characters took over and changed the game.It was only around somewhere HERE that I finally started pay actual attention to the plot.<br><br>Mystery,romance,pain and drama notched up so quickly I was left shocked and utterly impresssed at the way the writer decided to finish things.And that,my friends,was what lead me to give it a 4 star, It's end.<br><br><b>Recommended to anybody <s>with patience and</s> in need for a light-hearted action read.Nothing really memorable or worth re-reading :/ </b><br><br>(Oh and a word to all fans of the 'Chocolate lover' series out there ,This book is very different from those,and humor is defiantly not one of the genre I would use to describe this ....Just thought I'd let u lovlies know ! =) </span>
  <a data-text-id="11952091161999222496" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12003583461837839394">So, I wish I had never read this book. In e format, that is. I seriously had to keep going back to triple check that the author of this book was the same one that had me laughing myself to tears with her Chocolate Lover's series.   <span id="freeText12003583461837839394" style="display:none">So, I wish I had never read this book. In e format, that is. I seriously had to keep going back to triple check that the author of this book was the same one that had me laughing myself to tears with her Chocolate Lover's series. It's unfathomable how the same author wrote these books! This is a sign of pure freaking genius, to crossover with this level of success.<br /><br />With that out of the way, let me tell you that I lost myself in this book. Milo, Annabelle and Garrett are very solid characters with a very rich history that we get to explore randomly throughout the book, and quite deeply as well. The reader gets a real connection with these people and the friendship and love that exist. Once you start feeling and understanding their pasts, it all starts to fall apart. <br /><br />THEN...the Navy Seal/CIA type of mystery, investigation and intrigue start. If I was a betting gal, I would say that Sivec grew up reading those romance mystery novels because this novel had some old school romance intrigue feel. <br /><br />The gunfights, revelations by the bad guys and military type missions weren't overshadowed by the second guessing of true love and loyalties. There was A LOT going on in this book all the time and that made for a must read feel.<br /><br />I'm may have loved this book because of Tara's place on my fave author list and the fact my expectations were slanted because I wanted to love it out my high hopes for her. I notice from other reviews that this book was a hit with everyone though, no surprise. It was great!! <br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5409058093733129643">This novel was very long & very tedious, & I'm thankful that it's over.... When an author writes a romantic storyline involving the Navy Seals & government corruption, set against an international backdrop, he/she walks a fine line between excitement & cheesiness. And although I really enjoyed the first 40-50% of this novel, I'm sad to say that (for me) the novel quickly spiraled into cheesy trite territory. I commend the author for trying to write a romance novel with a complex storyline. Unfor</span>
  <span id="freeText5409058093733129643" style="display:none">This novel was very long &amp; very tedious, &amp; I'm thankful that it's over.... When an author writes a romantic storyline involving the Navy Seals &amp; government corruption, set against an international backdrop, he/she walks a fine line between excitement &amp; cheesiness. And although I really enjoyed the first 40-50% of this novel, I'm sad to say that (for me) the novel quickly spiraled into cheesy trite territory.     <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_469098594" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/469098594" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/469098594?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17155633-a-beautiful-lie">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer469098594" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6726399049217592017"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“If you were mine, I would never be able to walk away from you. If you were mine, I'd worship every inch of your body with my hands, lips, and tongue. If you were mine, I wouldn’t be able to stand in the same room as you without running my hands over your skin and tasting your lips. If you were mine…”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>Oh My… Never in a million years did I expect the woman who only recently left me in stitches and caused me to snort from laughter to now make my heart race and my skin tingle. This book </span>
  <span id="freeText6726399049217592017" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“If you were mine, I would never be able to walk away from you. If you were mine, I'd worship every inch of your body with my hands, lips, and tongue. If you were mine, I wouldn’t be able to stand in the same room as you without running my hands over your skin and tasting your lips. If you were mine…”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />Oh My… Never in a million years did I expect the woman who only recently left me in stitches and caused me to snort from laughter to now make my heart race and my skin tingle. This book was such a welcome but completely unexpected surprise – it took Ms Sivec out of the ‘funny box’ and catapulted her into any genre she damn wishes to write in. If I’ve learned anything from this book is that no one puts Tara in a ‘box’.<br /><br />This story starts as many others do – three best friends, a love triangle marked by years of unspoken feelings and regrets. Our heroine, Parker, is a young woman whose past conditioned her to believe that allowing herself to love someone completely and sharing all of herself with another would only lead to disappointment and a broken heart. She watched her own father fade away after the death of her mother, shattered and changed by the intense pain from losing the love of his life. Watching him turn his back on his own daughter scarred her deeply, but it also affected every relationship that Parker entered into after that, always keeping her distance and never allowing herself to love with all her heart.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“She swore she would never let someone take so much of her heart and soul that it would wither away to nothing once they were gone. She gave up on the dream of finding someone to consume her mind, body, and soul. It only ruined you in the end. It only left you broken and unable to live.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Garrett and Milo have been best friends since they were children, Garrett always taking the selfless role of protector and defender, and never once putting his own ambitions or dreams before Milo’s. He sees Parker first but he does not act on it because he notices his friend’s interest in her as well. For years he then watches his best friend with the woman of his dreams, silently wishing it was him sharing a life with her, compartmentalizing his feelings and turning a lie into his daily truth.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“He buried his feelings, his wants, and desires and stepped aside so his friend could finally find some peace and happiness.”</i>
</blockquote><br />When Parker meets Garrett and Milo, two young Navy SEALS recruits, in her first year of college, she inevitably goes for the one that doesn’t awaken her body and soul, the one that doesn’t make her heart skip a beat every time he looks at her. She starts a nice and easy relationship with Milo, the ‘safer’ one of the two, a relationship with no complications or expectations, one that progresses at a steady pace but leaves Parker free to keep her distance. Her friendship with Garrett, on the other hand, only grows over the years, making them each other’s confidante and shoulder to cry on, but they never cross that line where they would have to admit their feelings to each other. They both suppress their lingering thoughts about one another, the painful ‘what-ifs’, nurturing their friendship above all else.<br /><br />And then one day Milo gets killed under suspicious circumstances during a top-secret mission abroad.<br /><br />What follows is a fast-paced suspense-ridden adventure with secrets unveiled at every corner. We watch Parker and Garrett navigate through endless lies, struggle with what they discover about their friend’s death, but even more with what they are forced to admit to each other. Their chemistry sizzles, takes a life of its own, making this not only an exciting and suspenseful roller-coaster ride of a story, but also a seismic romance between two people who were never meant to be apart. They struggle with their feelings, question what their bodies won’t deny them, desperate to break through each other’s defences and find their happily-ever-after.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Garrett couldn’t get deep enough, couldn’t feel enough of her body. He wanted to drown in her and shout at the top of his lungs that she was his. It was always her, only her.”</i>
</blockquote><br />This was such a genre departure for this awesome author and she pulled it off beautifully. If I had to make a remark on anything that perhaps didn’t work so well for me it would be the number of ‘inner voices’ we get to hear throughout the story, even for the most secondary of characters. I would have also preferred more dialogues to be able to read the motivations behind a character’s actions, rather than to be told what they were. The narrative overtook the dialogues and that for me personally was overwhelming at times. But regardless of this, the writing style was mature and engaging, firmly cementing Ms Sivec as one of my favourite authors.<br /><br />If you are looking for a gripping, fast-moving, stimulating read that will keep you glued to the pages and squeal from delight, look no further. It is a beautiful lie indeed.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I know love isn’t something that comes easy for you or that you even believe in it. I know and I don’t care. I don’t care if you’re afraid to love me back, I don’t care if you never feel the same way that I do. I just need you to know, right here and right now, that I am in love with you, Annabelle Parker.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><b>[4.5 STARS}</b><br /><br />~ N ♥<br /><br /><a href="http://wp.me/p2YIUs-12R" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6726399049217592017" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_495706815" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/495706815" />
    <a title="Anne OK" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok"><img alt="Anne OK" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505981069p2/285610.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/495706815?book_show_action=true">Jan 04, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Anne OK" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Anne OK" href="/user/show/285610-anne-ok">Anne OK</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/285610-anne-ok?shelf=2013-reads">2013-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer495706815" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5478893655067067234">First time author for me – I have not read Tara Sivec’s “Chocolate Lovers Series” raved about by so many readers. I’m considering myself lucky that I don’t have to compare or fear the change in writing genres. Nope, this “beautiful” reading experience was only between the author T.E. Sivec and me. <br/> <br/>Before my applaud and cheers, I mention the only flaw that gave me pause. The division line between past and present in the third person writing style was a bit murky at times. I found myself returnin</span>
  <span id="freeText5478893655067067234" style="display:none">First time author for me – I have not read Tara Sivec’s “Chocolate Lovers Series” raved about by so many readers. I’m considering myself lucky that I don’t have to compare or fear the change in writing genres. Nope, this “beautiful” reading experience was only between the author T.E. Sivec and me. <br /> <br />Before my applaud and cheers, I mention the only flaw that gave me pause. The division line between past and present in the third person writing style was a bit murky at times. I found myself returning to a paragraph or page to make clear who was talking and was it from past or present day. I want to make clear that it didn’t disrupt long enough to ruin my enthusiasm for this book.<br /><br />This author has written a well-balanced combination of intrigue, suspense, and romance in “A Beautiful Lie.” With deceit and lies at the center of this story, three best friends find themselves in the middle of a passionate romantic triangle as well as an explosive “generational” secret military mission. Call in the FBI, the Navy SEALs and the CIA! The plot is filled with high octane action. There’s hardly a moment to catch your breath. And it’s really well-written and highly entertaining action. It almost felt like I was watching an action-packed thriller at the movies.<br /><br />Some reviewers have mentioned the slow build as a negative in the beginning where the plot and characters are being introduced. This slow burn had no adverse effect on this reader. It only enhanced the unfolding story and the well-developed construction of the characters. Sometimes the best things are worth the wait. As was the case here. <br /><br />A sweet and tender epilogue made for a perfect ending. Looking forward to Brady's story in the second book in Tivec's "Playing With Fire" series.<br /><br />Highly recommend. <br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="5478893655067067234" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/467574380?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer467574380" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13756048970882402303">Tara Sivec’s Chocolate Lovers series is one of the most entertaining series that I have read to date. So as soon as the first book of her new series was available I clicked purchased and jumped right in. <br/><br/>A Beautiful Lie is about as far from the Chocolate Lovers series as you can get. It definitely worked but was it for me? I think so I enjoyed it.<br/><br/>The story is told in the third person, which gives the reader the thoughts of all characters involved in this in depth story of navy seals, FBI agents,</span>
  <span id="freeText13756048970882402303" style="display:none">Tara Sivec’s Chocolate Lovers series is one of the most entertaining series that I have read to date. So as soon as the first book of her new series was available I clicked purchased and jumped right in. <br /><br />A Beautiful Lie is about as far from the Chocolate Lovers series as you can get. It definitely worked but was it for me? I think so I enjoyed it.<br /><br />The story is told in the third person, which gives the reader the thoughts of all characters involved in this in depth story of navy seals, FBI agents, CIA agents, crooked leaders and best friends.<br />The story line was a bit slow in the beginning but I couldn’t wait to uncover all the LIES so I read on. <br /><br />The two main characters Garrett (navy seal) and Parker (CIA agent), long time best friends decide to go undercover to find out what happened to Parker’s finance Milo in the Dominican. Garrett and Parker play newlyweds and all the feelings that the two have kept hidden are brought to the surface on their quest for the truth.<br /><br />My favorite character had to be Garrett I found that he was the most relatable as well as pretty hot.<br /><br />Truthfully, mystery novels aren’t my thing but the promise of romance held my attention throughout the book as well as the reveal of all secrets. I did enjoy the journey and it was a good read. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="13756048970882402303" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>
